<script type="text/javascript">

function validate_search()
{

	var form1 = document.frm1;
	var filter_mail=/^.+@.+\..{2,3}$/;
	if ((form1.search_val.value=="")||(form1.search_val.value=="Enter a Search Field"))
	{
		alert('Please enter a Search Field');
		form1.search_val.focus();
		return false;
	}

	if ((form1.category.value=="")||(form1.category.value=="Choose a Search Type"))
	{
		alert('Choose a Search Type');
		form1.category.focus();
		return false;
	}
	if ((form1.jtype.value=="")||(form1.jtype.value=="Enter a Search Field"))
	{
		alert('Choose a Journal Type');
		form1.jtype.focus();
		return false;
	}

	else
	{
		return true;
	}	

}

<!-- Contact Us Validation Start here -->
<script type="text/javascript">
function validate()

{
	var form = document.frm;
	var filter_mail=/^.+@.+\..{2,3}$/;
	if ((form.name.value=="")||(form.name.value=="Enter a name"))
	{

		alert('Please enter a Name');
		form.name.focus();
		return false;
	}

	else if ((form.email.value=="")||(form.email.value=="Enter a email id"))
	{
		alert('Please enter a Email-ID');
		form.email.focus();
		return false;

	}

	else if (!filter_mail.test(form.email.value))
	{
		alert('Please enter valid Email-ID');
		form.email.focus();
		return false;
	}

	else if ((form.comments.value=="")||(form.comments.value=="Enter a message"))
	{
		alert('Please enter your Message');
		form.comments.focus();
		return false;
	}

	else
	{
		return true;
	}	

}




function validate_email(id)
{
	var filter_mail=/^.+@.+\..{2,3}$/;
	if(id==1)
	var form = document.join_edit;
	else
	var form = document.join_reviewer;
	var emailID=form.mail.value;	
	if ((emailID=="")||(emailID=="Enter Your Email ID"))
	{

		alert('Please enter a Email-ID');
		form.mail.focus();
		return false;	
	}

	if(filter_mail.test(emailID))
	{
				return true;
	}
	else
	{
		alert('Please enter a valid Email-id');
		form.mail.focus();
		return false;

	}

}

</script>

<!-- Contact Us Validation End here -->

<script type="text/javascript">
function specialcharecter(txtName)
{
if (txtName.value != '' && txtName.value.match(/^[\w@. ]+$/) == null)



	{



		txtName.value = txtName.value.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9@. ]/g, ''); ///[\W\@\.]/g



	}


}

function allowonlydot(txtName)
{

	if (txtName.value != '' && txtName.value.match(/^[\w,.'" ]+$/) == null)

	{



		txtName.value = txtName.value.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9,.'" ]/g, ''); ///[\W\@\.]/g

	}



}
</script>

<script>
var div1 = $('.testimonial_con_2');
setInterval(function(){
    var pos1 = div1.scrollTop();
	
	 var scrollHeight1 = div1.prop("scrollHeight") - div1.height();
    if(pos1 < scrollHeight1)
    {
       div1.scrollTop(pos1 + 2);
    }
    else
    {
       div1.scrollTop(0);
    }
	
   
}, 200);
</script>
<script>
var div = $('.jou_list');
setInterval(function(){
    var pos = div.scrollTop();
	 var scrollHeight = div.prop("scrollHeight") - div.height();
    if(pos < scrollHeight)
    {
       div.scrollTop(pos + 2);
    }
    else
    {
       div.scrollTop(0);
    }
}, 200);



<!-- Auto scroll -->
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">


function RemoveSpecialChar1(txtName)
{

	if (txtName.value != '' && txtName.value.match(/^[\w-,@. ]+$/) == null)

	{



		txtName.value = txtName.value.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9-,@. ]/g, ''); ///[\W\@\.]/g



	}



}
function RemoveSpecialChar11(txtName)
{

	if (txtName.value != '' && txtName.value.match(/^[\w-,. ]+$/) == null)

	{



		txtName.value = txtName.value.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9-,. ]/g, ''); ///[\W\@\.]/g



	}



}



function GoCaptcha1111(site_path)



{



	//jQuery('#cvbvcb').html('<img src="loading.gif"/>');



	jQuery.ajax({



	type:"GET",



		url:'ajax_captcha111.php',



		dataType:"html",



		success: function(r){



			jQuery('#cvbvcb').html(r);



		}



	});



}

function allowNumberName11(txtName)
{

	if (txtName.value != '' && txtName.value.match(/^[\w ]+$/) == null)

	{



		txtName.value = txtName.value.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9 ]/g, ''); ///[\W\@\.]/g

	}



}


</script>
